<DESCRIPTION>EXHIBIT 99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; text-align: center"><IMG SRC="a.jpg" ALT="">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>MEGIDDO - JEZREEL VALLEY AREA</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>License Boundaries to be Published</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="color: #505050">This past Monday (May 20, 2013),
we submitted our final revised work plan in anticipation of the Petroleum Commissioner&rsquo;s meeting with Israel&rsquo;s nine-member
Petroleum Council to review Zion&rsquo;s application.</FONT><BR>
<BR>
<FONT STYLE="color: #505050">During&nbsp;<B>Israel&rsquo;s Petroleum Council meeting held this week</B>, Zion&rsquo;s license application
was discussed and they decided to announce (post official notice of) our proposed license area boundaries (approximately 98,000
acres in Israel&rsquo;s Megiddo and Jezreel Valley).</FONT><BR>
<BR>
<FONT STYLE="color: #505050">The announcement has since been posted to the Energy Ministry&rsquo;s&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="color: #EB4102"><B>website</B></FONT><FONT STYLE="color: #505050">.</FONT><BR>
<BR>
<FONT STYLE="color: #505050"><B>NOTE: This is a critically important step in the Energy Ministry&rsquo;s eventual license award
to Zion.</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 0pt; color: #505050">&nbsp;<IMG SRC="b.jpg" ALT=""></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">Zion&rsquo;s proposed 98,000
acre exploration license in the Megiddo-Jezreel Valley.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>Recent Israel Trip</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">In late April 2013, Dr. Lee Russell and I traveled
to Israel to meet with&nbsp;<B>Alexander Varshavsky (Israel&rsquo;s Petroleum Commissioner)</B>&nbsp;and Dr. Michael Gardosh (Director
of Geophysical Section) &ndash; both of Israel&rsquo;s Ministry of Energy and Water Resources.&nbsp;<BR>
<BR>
Together with Dr. Yehezkel &ldquo;Charlie&rdquo; Druckman (Zion&rsquo;s Liaison to the Energy Ministry), Ilan Sheena (Chief Financial
Officer), and Liat Shindler (Zion&rsquo;s geophysicist), we presented our corporate, financial, and geoscience case for our proposed
Megiddo-Jezreel License.&nbsp;<BR>
<BR>
Note the 200+ page notebook that contains our formal license application.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 0pt; color: #505050"><IMG SRC="c.jpg" ALT="">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">Presenting our case to Dr.
Gardosh and Petroleum Commissioner Varshavsky</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray"><IMG SRC="d.jpg" ALT="">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">From left to right, Ilan Sheena
(CFO), Petroleum Commissioner Varshavsky, Dr. Michael Gardosh, Victor Carrillo, Dr. Charlie Druckman, Dr. Lee Russell.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; color: gray">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">It was an incredibly worthwhile and useful exercise
as we received direct, immediate, and personal feedback from the two key people in the Energy Ministry that will be recommending
acceptance or rejection of our license.&nbsp;<BR>
<BR>
Since the meeting, we revised our work plan (which is the key item for which they suggested revisions) and Dr. Druckman continued
the dialogue with both Energy Ministry officials.&nbsp;<BR>
<BR>
Our recent decision to name Dr. Druckman, a former Israeli Petroleum Commissioner and a longtime Zion Board member, as our direct
contact with the Energy Ministry has been an excellent decision.&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>NEW GUIDELINES IN ISRAEL</B><BR>
<BR>
The new guidelines&nbsp;<B>require much more additional work</B>&nbsp;and corporate documentation than in prior years.<BR>
<BR>
The new evaluation process requires several months before the application can be approved.&nbsp; Our proposed license boundaries
must be published for at least three months to enable other companies the opportunity to submit a competing bid or offer for the
same area.<BR>
<BR>
We are only<B>&nbsp;the second company&nbsp;</B>to seek a new onshore license under these new guidelines.&nbsp; Earlier this year,
Genie Oil &amp; Gas received a license in the Golan Heights in a competitive bidding process.&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>Seismic Acquisition Planning</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><BR>
When our Megiddo-Jezreel Valley license is approved in a few months, we will still need to acquire new seismic data before we can
confirm our preliminary well site location for our first exploratory well there.<BR>
<BR>
Liat Shindler, our Israel-based geophysicist, has already launched a&nbsp;<B>seismic viability study&nbsp;</B>along with the Geophysical
Institute of Israel in the Megiddo and Jezreel Valley area.&nbsp;<BR>
<BR>
The seismic planning, acquisition, processing, and interpretation cycle can be a long process so we are getting a jumpstart on
the process even before we are granted the license.&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>Updates on our other Licenses</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><BR>
<B>ASHER - MENASHE LICENSE&nbsp;</B>(Elijah #3 Re-Entry Well)<BR>
<BR>
Today, May 23, 2013, we applied for the final one-year extension of the Asher-Menashe License to conduct final in-well testing
operations at the Elijah #3 well<B>&nbsp;in hopes of finding commercially productive hydrocarbons</B>.<BR>
<BR>
If testing operations prove negative, we plan to plug and decommission the well as required by our license terms.<BR>
<BR>
<B>JORDAN VALLEY LICENSE</B><BR>
<BR>
We recently entered into a contract with Geomage, an Israel-based geophysical company, to reprocess existing seismic lines in an
effort to improve our subsurface imaging ability in both the Jordan Valley and proposed Megiddo-Jezreel License areas.&nbsp;<BR>
<BR>
This effort will aid us in high-grading exploration leads in both areas to develop them into drillable prospects.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<BR>
<BR>
<B>JOSEPH LICENSE</B><BR>
<BR>
On May 12, 2013 we received official notice from the Petroleum Commissioner that our Joseph License extension request was granted
to October 10, 2013.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #505050"><B>Direct Stock Purchase Program</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><BR>

<BR>
